The dashboard schema version system supports versions 0-42, with version 42 being the final version for the v1 dashboard API.\\n\\n## Frontend Implementation\\n\\n### Main Migrator Class\\n**File**: `public/app/features/dashboard/state/DashboardMigrator.ts`\\n- **Key Export**: `DashboardMigrator` class with `updateSchema()` method\\n- **Schema Version Constant**: `DASHBOARD_SCHEMA_VERSION = 42`\\n- Contains all 42+ schema version migrations implemented as conditional blocks\\n- Includes field-level migration functions for specific transformations:\\n  - `upgradeToGridLayout()` - Migrates dashboard from row-based to grid layout (v16)\\n  - `migrateCloudWatchQueries()` - Handles CloudWatch metric query splitting\\n  - `migrateCloudWatchAnnotationQuery()` - Handles CloudWatch annotation query splitting\\n  - `upgradePanelLink()` - Migrates panel links\\n  - `migrateDatasourceNameToRef()` - Converts datasource names to reference objects\\n  - `upgradeValueMappings()` - Migrates value mapping structures\\n  - `migrateTooltipOptions()` - Renames tooltip configuration\\n  - `ensureXAxisVisibility()` - Preserves time axis visibility\\n  - `migrateHideFromFunctionality()` - Migrates field visibility overrides\\n- Handles panel-specific auto-migrations for deprecated panel types (singlestat→stat, graph→timeseries, etc.)\\n\\n## Backend Implementation\\n\\n### Main Migration Orchestrator\\n**File**: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/migrate.go`\\n- **Key Functions**:\\n  - `Initialize()` - Initializes migrator with datasource provider\\n  - `Migrate()` - Main entry point for dashboard JSON migration\\n- **Process Flow**:\\n  1. Cleans up dashboard properties not included in frontend save model\\n  2. Tracks original transformations and fieldConfig state\\n  3. Applies frontend defaults (DashboardModel and PanelModel)\\n  4. Ensures all panels have unique IDs\\n  5. Executes migration pipeline from current version to target version\\n  6. Adds built-in annotation query\\n  7. Cleans up dashboard for save (removes defaults and non-persisted properties)\\n\\n### Frontend Defaults Application\\n**File**: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/frontend_defaults.go`\\n- **Key Functions**:\\n  - `applyFrontendDefaults()` - Applies DashboardModel constructor defaults\\n  - `applyPanelDefaults()` - Applies PanelModel constructor defaults\\n  - `ensurePanelsHaveUniqueIds()` - Ensures unique panel IDs\\n  - `cleanupDashboardForSave()` - Removes non-persisted properties\\n  - `cleanupPanelForSaveWithContext()` - Cleans individual panels\\n  - `applyPanelAutoMigration()` - Handles deprecated panel type auto-migration\\n  - `getGraphAutoMigration()` - Special logic for graph panel migration\\n  - `removeNullValuesRecursively()` - Matches frontend JSON.stringify behavior\\n\\n### Schema Version Migration Registry\\n**File**: `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/schemaversion/migrations.go`\\n- **Key Functions**:\\n  -
